< Pictures>
[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN2O9uv3yHK6BlEOOEy5Fi1B0KE3e06a78InExM=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pictures>
<gmapID>0x80dca798c075ad91:0x6e7767c801a938f6<//gmapID>< text>
I've been twice to the new one that just opened in eastern Moreno Valley, CA, near the super target off of Nason. I had heard of the store but had not been in one prior to these visits.

Both times, upon entering, the employees were friendly and welcoming with offers to help find what I was looking for.

It's new, so the store was clean and shelves well stocked.

I told my family that it's going to be a useful place to have so close to our house.

There's such a varied amount of things in there I compared it to having a mini auto parts store, pet store, clothing store, tool store, home decor store (if you like country decor) etc. I was, frankly, amazed at the variety of things they had and the store wasn't that big, all things considered.

It is designed to make country living easier with products that you would need to work on tractors and other machinery. I saw the biggest wrench I'd ever seen there, so it's covering some really big equipment!

You don't need to have a farm/ranch life to be able to find something for suburban living. They ran the gamut with pets, from to birds, cats and dogs and their supplies, so the way up to horses and cows and several critters inbetween!

I'll just say if you haven't seen one it's worth taking a look at. I'm not that great at price comparison so I can't tell you if it compares to another store, but they are close by so it may save a run across town.<//text>

<user_name>David Good<//user_name>< Response>
None< /Response>
< review>
This is a comfortable place -- nice atmosphere with excellent food.  I've been here several times while traveling for work... each time having something a bit different... and each time I have been extremely pleased with the quality of the food.  Some of the best chicken alfredo I've had.

It was a fluke that brought me here.  If I had just been walking by this restaurant and poked my head in the door, I probably would have just left.  While it is certainly clean and modern inside, the feel of the dining area just reminds me too much of the dining area of a Luby's or other cafeteria-style restaurants.  It's all in my head, I know, but I guess I'm just not a fan of the "block" style seating, and the "modern" furniture (I like to see big, old tables made of wood with tablecloths that are all positioned at a 45 degree angle from each other... so you're never sitting block-style (or shoulder-to-shoulder) with the table next to you.  Again -- this is just a mental thing for me, not necessarily a flaw.  I'm sure most other people could care less how the floor layout is.  I'm just saying that if I were walking by, it would have been a turn-off for me and I might not have given the restaurant a proper try.

Fortunately, I was with another co-worker at the time and pretty much had no choice but to go in and try the place out (I wasn't willing to not give it a try, since we both drove out to the location on a recommendation).  I'm glad I gave it a chance -- because it was excellent.  The food was so good, that I would have ordered a second plate if I were alone and had the time (or if my co-worker wanted a second plate as well).  It's a good thing I didn't order a second plate, as I would have been hurting -- but the food was so good I really wanted more.  And I remembered that feeling, which is why I've been back several times -- each time with another co-worker.

The outside seating is nice if it's not too breezy or cold out.

They have a good selection of wine, beer, etc., and the wait staff was friendly.  On one visit the waiter didn't seem to pay us enough attention (which was odd, considering it wasn't crowded at all at that time) but the staff has been quick all other times I've been there.

I can't say I'll ever love the layout of the dining area -- it has a "quick lunch" feel, not a "sit down and take your time at dinner" feel.  For that reason, I can't give them five stars (atmosphere is an important part of the entire experience for me).  But the food will keep me coming back.<//review>
